id=loadError.label
en=Page load error
tr=頁面載入錯誤

id=retry.label
en=Try again
tr=重試

id=protocolNotFound.longDesc
en=The address (URL) starts with a protocol that is not recognized by the browser. A protocol is the part at the front of the address, such as http: or ftp: which tells the browser how to connect to the site. In this instance, the protocol is unknown so loading cannot continue. Check that the address is correct before retrying.
tr=網址（URL）指定的通訊協定無法辨視。通訊協定指的是網址開頭的部份，像 http: 或 ftp: 。請檢查你的網址是否正確。

id=connectionFailure.title
en=Connection Failure Error
tr=連線失敗

id=connectionFailure.longDesc
en=The browser was unable to connect to the specified site, even though it exists. This may be because the site does not accept connections from your computer, the service may be down, or the site does not support the service or port that you tried to connect to.
tr=連線失敗，不過網站存在。可能該網站拒絕你的電腦的連線，或是目前無法服務等問題。

id=netTimeout.title
en=Net Timeout Error
tr=網路逾時

id=netTimeout.longDesc
en=The browser timed out while trying to connect to the specified site. The site may be experiencing high loads that are slowing it down, or network problems are preventing data from being received from it in a timely manner. If the site is likely to be busy, consider waiting a few moments before retrying the request.
tr=瀏覽器連線等待時間過久（timeout）。或許該網站目前流量過高，或網路發生問題。請稍候再試。

id=redirectLoop.title
en=Redirect Loop Error
tr=重新導向(Redirect)發生迴圈

id=redirectLoop.longDesc
en=The browser has stopped a connection because the site is redirecting requests to itself in a manner which prevents it from ever completing.
tr=重新導向(Redirect)發生迴圈

id=unknownSocketType.title
en=Unknown Socket Error
tr=未知的Socket錯誤

id=unknownSocketType.longDesc
en=The site responded to the network request in an unexpected manner. This may be due to address (URL) using the wrong protocol for the specified port, or a non-standard configuration on the site which is running different services than expected.
tr=網站回應錯誤。可能是網址（URL）使用了錯誤的通訊協定，或網站服務設定有誤。

id=netReset.title
en=Net Reset Error
tr=網路重設

id=generic.longDesc
en=The page could not be loaded, possibly because it does not exist or the location is incorrect.<br/>Check that the address (URL) is valid and correctly formatted.
tr=頁面無法載入，可能是網頁不存在或網址錯誤。<br/>請檢查網址（URL）是否正確。

tr=網路連線被中斷，可能是中間的網路有問題。如果此問題持續發生，請聯絡系統管理員。

id=malformedURI.longDesc
en=The address (URL) is not a valid format and cannot be read. A typical address will start with &quot;http://&quot;, followed by an address, (e.g. www.netscape.com), followed by a path to the content (or just &quot;/&quot;). A common cause for the problem is using backslashes(\\) instead of forward slashes (/).
tr=網址（URL）不正確。通常正確的網址會用「http://」開始，接著一個位址（如 www.mozilla.org），再接一段路經（如只有「/」）。常見的錯誤是用了倒斜線（\\），請改用斜線（/）。

In such cases you should consult your system documentation, administrator or Internet Service Provider (ISP) as appropriate for further assistance.
tr=網址（URL）指定的電腦名稱不存在。如果你確定沒打錯，可能是你的 Proxy 或 DNS 設定有誤。請詢問你的系統管理員或 ISP。
